"SELECT `training_times`.`id`, `date`, DATE_FORMAT(`time_start`, '%H:%i') as time_start, `length`, DATE_FORMAT(`time_end`, '%H:%i') as time_end, `hall`, `trainer`, `training_name`, `color`,\nWEEKDAY(`date`) as `weekday`, WEEK(`date`,1) as `week` \nFROM `training_times` JOIN (`trainings`) ON (`trainings`.`id` = `training_id`) \nWHERE WEEK(`date`,1) = WEEK('2011-04-15',1)   AND `hall` = '1' ORDER BY `date` "
